namespace = DG_Catholics
country_event = { 
	id = DG_Catholics.001
	title = "DG_Catholics.001.title"
	desc = "DG_Catholics.001.desc"
	picture = all_church_state
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = { 
		is_religion_enabled = protestant
		religion_years = { 
			protestant = 35
		}
		tag = PAP
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		years = 25
	}
	immediate = { 
		set_global_flag = counter_reformation
		set_country_flag = catholic_revival
		log = "DG:[GetYear]:2530:Counter_Reformation:Birth:Rome:[This.GetName]"
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.001.opta"
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_known_country = { 
				limit = { 
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { 
						has_country_flag = catholic_revival
					}
					NOT = { 
						has_country_flag = religious_compromise
					}
				}
				country_event = { 
					id = DG_Catholics.002
					days = 45
					random = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						which = opw
						value = 10
					}
				}
				add_country_modifier = { 
					name = dg_rc_10
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_20
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_30
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_40
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_50
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_60
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_70
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_80
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_90
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					check_variable = { 
						which = opw
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_10
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_20
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_30
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_40
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_50
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_60
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_70
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_80
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_90
			}
			else = { 
				set_variable = { 
					which = opw
					value = 0
				}
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_10
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_20
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_30
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_40
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_50
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_60
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_70
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_80
				remove_country_modifier = dg_rc_90
			}
			add_opinion = { 
				who = PAP
				modifier = papacy_bad
			}
		}
	}
	after = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				any_country = { 
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { 
						has_country_flag = catholic_revival
					}
					NOT = { 
						has_country_flag = religious_compromise
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { 
				random_known_country = { 
					limit = { 
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { 
							has_country_flag = catholic_revival
						}
						NOT = { 
							has_country_flag = religious_compromise
						}
					}
					country_event = { 
						id = DG_Catholics.002
						days = 45
						random = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_emperor = yes
				has_dlc = "Art of War"
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					any_known_country = { 
						AND = { 
							government = republic
							has_reform = Pol_Mandate1
							has_reform = Pol_Stylings1
							has_reform = Pol_ExtraPowers1
							has_reform = Pol_Assembly2
							has_reform = Pol_TermOfOffice5
							has_reform = free_city
						}
						religion = ROOT
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { 
					random_province = { 
						limit = { 
							is_part_of_hre = yes
							owner = { 
								AND = { 
									government = republic
									has_reform = Pol_Mandate1
									has_reform = Pol_Stylings1
									has_reform = Pol_ExtraPowers1
									has_reform = Pol_Assembly2
									has_reform = Pol_TermOfOffice5
									has_reform = free_city
								}
								religion = ROOT
							}
						}
						province_event = { 
							id = DG_Catholics.010
							days = 365
							random = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = { 
				hidden_effect = { 
					random_province = { 
						limit = { 
							is_part_of_hre = yes
							religion = ROOT
						}
						province_event = { 
							id = DG_Catholics.010
							days = 365
							random = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				BOH = { 
					religion = hussite
				}
				NOT = { 
					any_known_country = { 
						NOT = { 
							tag = BOH
						}
						religion = hussite
					}
				}
			}
			BOH = { 
				country_event = { 
					id = DG_Catholics.003
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				AND = { 
					hre_religion = protestant
					religion = protestant
				}
				AND = { 
					hre_religion = reformed
					religion = reformed
				}
				AND = { 
					hre_religion = hussite
					religion = hussite
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
		}
		add_papal_influence = 25
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				is_elector = yes
				NOT = { 
					religion = reformed
				}
				NOT = { 
					overlord = { 
						religion = reformed
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_fanatical
			}
		}
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				capital_scope = { 
					is_part_of_hre = yes
				}
				NOT = { 
					religion = reformed
				}
				OR = { 
					is_elector = no
					overlord = { 
						religion = reformed
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_pious
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.013.optd"
		trigger = { 
			hre_religion_treaty = yes
			OR = { 
				AND = { 
					hre_religion = catholic
					OR = { 
						religion = protestant
						religion = reformed
						religion = hussite
					}
				}
				AND = { 
					hre_religion = protestant
					OR = { 
						religion = catholic
						religion = reformed
						religion = hussite
					}
				}
				AND = { 
					hre_religion = reformed
					OR = { 
						religion = protestant
						religion = catholic
						religion = hussite
					}
				}
				AND = { 
					hre_religion = hussite
					OR = { 
						religion = protestant
						religion = reformed
						religion = catholic
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 15
		}
		set_hre_religion_treaty = no
		add_imperial_influence = -50
		add_papal_influence = 25
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				religion = catholic
			}
			set_hre_religion = catholic
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				religion = protestant
			}
			set_hre_religion = protestant
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				religion = hussite
			}
			set_hre_religion = hussite
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				religion = reformed
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						is_religion_enabled = reformed
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { 
					enable_religion = reformed
				}
			}
			set_hre_religion = reformed
		}
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				is_elector = yes
				NOT = { 
					religion = reformed
				}

					overlord = { 
						religion = reformed
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_fanatical
			}
		}
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				capital_scope = { 
					is_part_of_hre = yes
				}
				NOT = { 
					religion = reformed
				}
				OR = { 
					is_elector = no
					overlord = { 
						religion = reformed
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_pious
			}
		}
	}
	after = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_country = { 
				limit = { 
					capital_scope = { 
						is_part_of_hre = yes
					}
					AND = { 
						OR = { 
							is_subject = no
							is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
							is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
							is_subject_of_type = muscovite_tributary_state
						}
					}
					hre_heretic_religion = ROOT
					NOT = { 
						emperor = { 
							religion = ROOT
						}
					}
					hre_religion_treaty = no
					is_emperor = no
				}
				country_event = { 
					id = DG_Catholics.014
					days = 95
					random = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}

							}

							}
							emperor = {

							}

							}
						}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { 
	id = DG_Catholics.026
	title = "DG_Catholics.026.title"
	desc = "DG_Catholics.026.desc"
	picture = protestant_league_war
	trigger = { 
		emperor = { 
			is_in_league_war = yes
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_global_flag = first_league_war
		}
		OR = { 
			AND = { 
				ai = no
				is_league_leader = yes
			}
			is_emperor = yes
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		set_global_flag = first_league_war
		set_global_flag = league_war
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					hre_religion = catholic
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_catholic
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					hre_religion = protestant
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_protestant
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					hre_religion = hussite
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_hussite
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					hre_religion = reformed
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_reformed
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					any_country = { 
						in_league = protestant
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_protestant
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					any_country = { 
						in_league = hussite
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_hussite
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					any_country = { 
						in_league = reformed
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_reformed
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					any_country = { 
						in_league = catholic
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = hre_leagues_catholic
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					any_known_country = { 
						capital_scope = { 
							is_part_of_hre = yes
						}
						NOT = { 
							num_of_cities = 2
						}
						is_emperor = no
						is_elector = no
					}
				}
				random_country = { 
					limit = { 
						capital_scope = { 
							is_part_of_hre = yes
						}
						NOT = { 
							num_of_cities = 2
						}
						is_emperor = no
						is_elector = no
					}
					capital_scope = { 
						save_global_event_target_as = imperial_diet_of_augsburg
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						any_known_country = { 
							capital_scope = { 
								is_part_of_hre = yes
							}
							NOT = { 
								num_of_cities = 2
							}
							is_emperor = no
							is_elector = no
						}
					}
				}
				emperor = { 
					capital_scope = { 
						save_global_event_target_as = imperial_diet_of_augsburg
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.026.opta"
	}
}

					any_known_country = { 
						capital_scope = { 
							is_part_of_hre = yes
						}
						NOT = { 
							num_of_cities = 2
						}
						is_emperor = no
						is_elector = no
					}
				}
				random_country = { 
					limit = { 
						capital_scope = { 
							is_part_of_hre = yes
						}
						NOT = { 
							num_of_cities = 2
						}
						is_emperor = no
						is_elector = no
					}
					capital_scope = { 
						save_global_event_target_as = imperial_diet_of_augsburg
					}
				}
			}
			else = { 
				emperor = { 
					capital_scope = { 
						save_global_event_target_as = imperial_diet_of_augsburg
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.028.optc"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
		}
		add_dip_power = -25
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = DG_Catholics.036
	title = "DG_Catholics.036.title"
	desc = "DG_Catholics.036.desc"
	picture = protestant_league_peace
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.036.opta"
		event_target:imperial_diet_of_augsburg = { 
			set_variable = { 
				which = imperial_vote_catholic
				which = imperial_vote_religion_catholic
			}
			set_variable = { 
				which = imperial_vote_protestant
				which = imperial_vote_religion_protestant
			}
			set_variable = { 
				which = imperial_vote_hussite
				which = imperial_vote_religion_hussite
			}
			set_variable = { 
				which = imperial_vote_reformed
				which = imperial_vote_religion_reformed
			}
			set_variable = { 
				which = imperial_vote_tolerance
				which = imperial_vote_religion_tolerance
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						is_variable_equal = { 
							which = imperial_vote_religion
							value = 0
						}
					}
				}
				divide_variable = { 
					which = imperial_vote_religion_catholic
					which = imperial_vote_religion
				}
				divide_variable = { 
					which = imperial_vote_religion_protestant
					which = imperial_vote_religion
				}

				}

					which = imperial_vote_religion
				}
			}
		}

		set_global_flag = leagues_peace_of_westphalia

country_event = { 
	id = DG_Catholics.041
	title = "DG_Catholics.041.title"
	desc = "DG_Catholics.041.desc"
	picture = protestant_league_surrender
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = hre_leagues_catholic
				has_global_flag = hre_leagues_protestant
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					event_target:imperial_diet_of_augsburg = { 
						check_variable = { 
							which = imperial_vote_tolerance
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = vote_results_cath_prot
			}
			else = { 
				custom_tooltip = vote_results_cath_prot_only
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = hre_leagues_catholic
				has_global_flag = hre_leagues_reformed
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					event_target:imperial_diet_of_augsburg = { 
						check_variable = { 
							which = imperial_vote_tolerance
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = vote_results_cath_ref
			}
			else = { 
				custom_tooltip = vote_results_cath_ref_only
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = hre_leagues_reformed
				has_global_flag = hre_leagues_protestant
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					event_target:imperial_diet_of_augsburg = { 
						check_variable = { 
							which = imperial_vote_tolerance
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = vote_results_ref_prot
			}
			else = { 
				custom_tooltip = vote_results_ref_prot_only
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = DG_Catholics.041.not_over_yet
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_variable = { 
				which = imperial_votes
				value = 0
			}
			clr_country_flag = imperial_diet_voted_religion
			country_event = { 
				id = DG_Catholics.045
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				hre_religion = catholic
				hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
			tooltip = { 
				set_hre_religion = catholic
				set_hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				hre_religion = protestant
				hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
			tooltip = { 
				set_hre_religion = protestant
				set_hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				hre_religion = hussite
				hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
			tooltip = { 
				set_hre_religion = hussite
				set_hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				hre_religion = reformed
				hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
			tooltip = { 
				set_hre_religion = reformed
				set_hre_religion_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.041.good"
		trigger = { 
			hre_religion = ROOT
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_emperor = yes
			}
			add_imperial_influence = 100
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 40
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 30
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 20
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_emperor = no
				capital_scope = { 
					is_part_of_hre = yes
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 20
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 15
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 10
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.041.bad"
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				hre_religion = ROOT
			}
			OR = { 
				AND = { 
					religion = catholic
					has_global_flag = hre_leagues_catholic
				}
				AND = { 
					religion = protestant
					has_global_flag = hre_leagues_protestant
				}
				AND = { 
					religion = reformed
					has_global_flag = hre_leagues_reformed
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_emperor = yes
			}
			add_imperial_influence = -100
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -40
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -30
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -20
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_emperor = no
				capital_scope = { 
					is_part_of_hre = yes
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -20
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = 0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -15
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.20
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -10
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						piety = -0.60
					}
				}
				add_prestige = -5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.041.neutral"
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				hre_religion = ROOT
			}
			NOT = { 
				OR = { 
					AND = { 
						religion = catholic
						has_global_flag = hre_leagues_catholic
					}
					AND = { 
						religion = protestant
						has_global_flag = hre_leagues_protestant
					}
					AND = {

						has_global_flag = hre_leagues_reformed
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

province_event = { 
	id = DG_Catholics.118
	title = "DG_Catholics.118.title"
	desc = "DG_Catholics.118.desc"
	picture = ANGLICAN_SERMON_eventPicture
	trigger = { 
		has_global_flag = counter_reformation
		is_religion_enabled = protestant
		has_province_flag = printing_press_p
		NOT = { 
			is_institution_enabled = Global_Trade
		}
		AND = { 
			continent = europe
			religion = catholic
			NOT = { 
				province_id = 2530
			}
			is_reformation_center = no
			is_island = no
			expelling_minorities = no
			development = 15
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					is_reformation_center = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				any_province = { 
					superregion = PREV
					is_reformation_center = yes
					religion = catholic
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_climate = tropical
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_climate = arid
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_climate = arctic
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_terrain = arctic
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_terrain = taiga
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_terrain = tundra
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 90
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.50
			has_country_flag = catholic_revival
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.50
			province_id = 2530
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.75
			is_capital = yes
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.90
			superregion = france_superregion
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.50
			superregion = italy_superregion
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.50
			superregion = iberia_superregion
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 1.50
			superregion = germany_superregion
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.75
			superregion = greater_austrian_circle_superregion
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 1.25
			superregion = balkan_superregion
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.95
			superregion = commonwealth_superregion
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 1.50
			superregion = scandinavian_superregion
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.118.opta"
		trigger = { 
			owner = { 
				religion = catholic
			}
		}
		add_reform_center = catholic
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_province_modifier = religious_enthusiasm
			}
			extend_province_modifier = { 
				name = religious_enthusiasm
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		else = { 
			add_province_modifier = { 
				name = religious_enthusiasm
				duration = 3650
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Catholics.118.optb"
		trigger = { 
			owner = { 
				NOT = { 
					religion = catholic
				}
			}
		}
		add_reform_center = catholic
